WHERE regime='bull' AND strategy='proc'`）\n- 比 JSON 小 60%（预估 600-800MB vs 1.8GB JSON）\n- 单文件好管理，支持事务（中断可恢复）\n\n## 数据库 Schema\n\n```sql\n-- 1. 汇总表（~1720 行）\nCREATE TABLE combo_summary (\n    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,\n    strategy TEXT, coin TEXT, interval TEXT,\n    total_return REAL, final_balance REAL,\n    max_drawdown REAL, sharpe_ratio REAL, sortino_ratio REAL, calmar_ratio REAL,\n    total_trades INTEGER, winning_trades INTEGER, losing_trades INTEGER,\n    win_rate REAL, avg_win_pct REAL, avg_loss_pct REAL, profit_factor REAL,\n    ttp_count INTEGER,\n    double_count INTEGER, fastest_double_days REAL, avg_double_days REAL,\n    daily_open_positions REAL\n);\n\n-- 2. 配对交易表（~850万行，核心数据）\nCREATE TABLE paired_trades (\n    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,\n    combo_id INTEGER REFERENCES combo_summary(id),\n    open_candle_idx INTEGER,    -- K线索引（用于精确定位）\n    close_candle_idx INTEGER,\n    open_time TEXT,             -- '%Y-%m-%d'\n    close_time TEXT,\n    holding_bars INTEGER,       -- 持仓K线数\n    direction TEXT,             -- 'long' / 'short'\n    entry_price REAL,\n    exit_price REAL,\n    capital REAL,               -- 下注本金\n    position_size REAL,         -- capital × leverage\n    pnl REAL,\n    r_value REAL,               -- pnl / capital\n    balance_after REAL,\n    close_type TEXT,            -- 'ttp' / 'stop_loss' / 'signal' / 'liquidation' / 'end_of_data'\n    regime_at_open TEXT         -- 'bull' / 'bear' / 'ranging' / 'unknown'\n);\nCREATE INDEX idx_pt_combo ON paired_trades(combo_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_pt_regime ON paired_trades(regime_at_open);\n\n-- 3. Regime 时间线（~67万行，每根K线的regime标签）\nCREATE TABLE regime_timeline (\n    coin TEXT, interval TEXT,\n    candle_idx INTEGER,\n    candle_time_ms INTEGER,     -- 毫秒时间戳\n    regime TEXT,\n    adx REAL, sma_direction TEXT\n);\nCREATE UNIQUE INDEX idx_rt ON regime_timeline(coin, interval, candle_idx);\n\n-- 4. 运行元数据\nCREATE TABLE run_metadata (key TEXT PRIMARY KEY, value TEXT);\n```\n\n## 需要改的文件（2个）\n\n### 1. `src/backtest/backtest.py` — 最小改动\n\n**a) `__init__` 加 `candles` 参数**（避免重复从磁盘加载）：\n```python\ndef __init__(self, ..., candles: List[Dict] = None):\n    ...\n    if candles is not None:\n        self.candles = candles\n    else:\n        self.candles = self._load_data()\n```\n\n**b) 追踪每笔交易的 K 线索引**：\n```python\nself.trade_candle_indices: List[int] = []\n```\n在每个 `self.trades.append(...)` 处同时 `self.trade_candle_indices.append(i)`。\n约 15 处需要加（所有 Trade append 点）。\n\n### 2. 新建 `src/backtest/generate_seed.py` — 种子生成脚本\n\n## 脚本结构\n\n```\ngenerate_seed.py\n├── build_regime_timeline(klines, interval, config)\n│   → 独立函数，复制 RegimeStrategy 的滞后逻辑\n│   → 不实例化任何 Strategy 子类\n│   → 输入 K 线，输出每根的 regime 标签\n│\n├── pair_trades(trades, candle_indices, regime_timeline, leverage)\n│   → 将原始 Trade 配对（open + close = 1笔完整交易）\n│   → 计算 R 值、查找 regime 标签、判断平仓类型\n│\n├── save_to_db(db, combo_summary, paired_trades, regime_timeline)\n│   → SQLite 批量写入\n│\n└── main()\n    → 三层循环：coin(10) → interval(4) → strategy(43)\n    → 每个 (coin, interval) 只加载一次 K 线 + 计算一次 regime\n    → 43 个策略共享同一份 regime 标签\n```\n\n## 循环顺序（关键优化）\n\n```\nfor coin in COINS:                    # 10\n    for interval in INTERVALS:        # 4\n        candles = load_once()         # ← 只加载一次\n        regime = compute_once()       # ← 只算一次（~67秒/1m）\n        save_regime_to_db()\n\n        for strategy in STRATEGIES:   # 43\n            engine = BacktestEngine(candles=candles, ...)\n            result = engine.run_backtest(strategy)\n            paired = pair_trades(result.trades, ...)\n            save_to_db(paired)\n\n        db.commit()                   # 每 (coin,interval) 提交一次\n```\n\n## 交易配对算法\n\n```python\nopen_trade = None\npaired = []\nfor i, trade in enumerate(trades):\n    if trade.order_type in ('BUY', 'SELL'):\n        open_trade = (trade, candle_indices[i])\n    elif trade.order_type in ('CLOSE_BUY','CLOSE_SELL','TTP_CLOSE_BUY','TTP_CLOSE_SELL','LIQUIDATION'):\n        if open_trade:\n            direction = 'long' if open_trade[0].order_type == 'BUY' else 'short'\n            close_type = classify_close(trade)  # ttp/stop_loss/signal/liquidation\n            r_value = trade.pnl / open_trade[0].capital\n            regime = regime_timeline[open_trade[1]]['regime']\n            paired.append({...})\n            open_trade = None\n```\n\n平仓类型判定：\n- `TTP_CLOSE_*` → 'ttp'\n- `LIQUIDATION` → 'liquidation'\n- `CLOSE_*` 且 pnl ≈ -capital → 'stop_loss'（止损PnL = -capital×leverage×stop_loss_pct = -capital）\n- 其他 `CLOSE_*` → 'signal'\n\n## Regime 时间线计算\n\n独立函数，逻辑等价于 `RegimeStrategy` 但不加载子策略：\n\n1. `detector.detect_with_details(window)` → ADX + SMA方向\n2. 滞后阈值：趋势中 ADX<18 才退出，ranging 中 ADX>25 才进入趋势\n3. 禁止 bull↔bear 直接翻转（必须经过 ranging）\n4. min_dwell_bars=48 + confirm_bars=6\n5. ADX 周期按 interval 缩放：1m→48, 5m→32, 15m→28, 1h→14\n\n## 运行时间估算\n\n| 阶段 | 时间 | 说明 |\n|------|------|------|\n| K线加载（40次） | ~20秒 | OS缓存后快 |\n| Regime计算（40次） | ~15分钟 | 1m数据主要耗时 |\n| 回测（1720组） | ~45分钟 | 与当前持平 |\n| 配对+写入DB | ~5分钟 | 批量INSERT |\n| **总计** | **~65分钟** | |\n\n## 验证方案\n\n1. 跑完后检查：`SELECT COUNT(*) FROM paired_trades` → 应有~850万行\n2. 抽查一个 combo：对比 `paired_trades` 的汇总 vs `combo_summary` 的指标\n3. Regime 分布检查：`SELECT regime, COUNT(*) FROM regime_timeline GROUP BY regime`\n4. 跑一个 regime 分析查询，验证数据可用性\n\n## 种子报告能回答的问题（不用重跑）\n\n- 每个策略在 bull/bear/ranging 下的表现 → **数据驱动 regime_map**\n- 不同注码方式（固定/复利/Kelly）的模拟 → 从 R 值重算\n- TTP 有效性分析（按 regime/策略/持仓时长）\n- 止损触发率 vs 信号平仓率\n- 持仓时间与收益关系\n\n\nIf you need specific details from before exiting plan mode (like exact code snippets, error messages, or content you generated), read the full transcript at: /Users/allenbot/.claude/projects/-Users-allenbot/e30cab2f-c5ea-4eb4-b625-4710b6e81a05.jsonl"},"uuid":"3f07d1a0-07c1-4242-b2ef-c9977c87a6a7","timestamp":"2026-02-27T03:48:26.743Z","planContent":"# 文档更新 + 种子报告实现计划\n\n## Context\n\n**Phase A（先做）**：用户要求先更新 CHECKPOINT.md、CLAUDE.md/README.md，推送到 GitHub。\n当前 git 有大量未提交改动：backtest.py（固定注码+翻倍指标）、run_full_matrix.py（全矩阵回测v2）、regime v2（ADX三层复合+滞后阈值）、CHECKPOINT.md（新文件）。\n\n**Phase B（后做）**：生成**完整种子报告**（SQLite），包含：\n1. 汇总指标（已有）\n2. 每笔交易明细（开仓→平仓配对，含入场价/出场价/PnL/R值）\n3. 每笔交易的 regime 标签（开仓时刻的 bull/bear/ranging）\n\n目的：**一次跑完，以后所有分析直接从种子读取，永远不用重跑回测。**\n\n用户原则：追求完整性、真实性、准确性。\n\n---\n\n## Phase A：文档更新 + GitHub 推送\n\n### A1. 更新 CHECKPOINT.md\n\n改动要点：\n- 任务 7 \"整合指标进交易系统\" → ✅ 已完成（Regime v2 ADX 三层实现 + MarketScore 辅助）\n- 新增任务 8 ✅ \"全矩阵回测 v2\"（1720组固定注码，含翻倍指标）\n- 新增任务 9 ⬜ \"种子报告\"（当前目标，详细方案见下方 Phase B）\n- 删除\"等待 Sonnet 出详细实施方案\"等过时内容\n- 更新版本号为 v1.7\n\n### A2. 更新 CLAUDE.md\n\n改动要点：\n- Backtest System 部分加入：固定注码模式（fixed_bet）、翻倍时间指标、`run_full_matrix.py` 全矩阵脚本\n- 加入 Regime Detection v2 说明（ADX 三层复合 + 滞后阈值）\n- 版本号更新\n\n### A3. 更新 README.md\n\n改动要点：\n- 目录结构加入 `run_full_matrix.py`、regime/ 目录\n- 新增 2.11 Regime Detection 章节\n- 新增 5.4 全矩阵回测说明\n- 更新日志加 v1.7\n- 版本号更新\n\n### A4. combo_summary(strategy, coin, interval);\n\"\"\"\n\n\n# ==================== K 线加载 ====================\n\ndef load_candles(coin: str, interval: str) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"加载 K 线数据（完整文件，不截取）\"\"\"\n    data_file = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'historical', coin, f'{interval}.json')\n    if not os.path.exists(data_file):\n        return []\n    with open(data_file, 'r') as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\n\n# ==================== Regime 时间线计算 ====================\n\ndef compute_regime_timeline(candles: List[Dict], interval: str,\n                            days: int) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"计算每根 K 线的 regime 标签\n\n    复制 RegimeStrategy 的滞后逻辑（_apply_hysteresis + _maybe_switch），\n    但不实例化任何子策略。\n\n    Returns:\n        列表，每个元素 = {candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction}\n    \"\"\"\n    bars_per_day_map = {\n        '1m': 1440, '5m': 288, '15m': 96, '30m': 48,\n        '1h': 24, '2h': 12, '4h': 6, '1d': 1,\n    }\n    bars_per_day = bars_per_day_map.get(interval, 24)\n\n    n = len(candles)\n    start_idx = max(0, n - days * bars_per_day)\n\n    # 配置\n    adx_period = get_adx_period(interval)\n    cfg = RegimeDetectorConfig(adx_period=adx_period)\n    detector = MarketRegimeDetector(cfg)\n\n    MAX_WINDOW = 200\n\n    # 滞后状态\n    current_regime = \"unknown\"\n    regime_bars = 0\n    pending_regime = None\n    pending_count = 0\n\n    timeline = []\n\n    for i in range(start_idx, n):\n        window_start = max(0, i + 1 - MAX_WINDOW)\n        window = candles[window_start:i + 1]\n\n        if len(window) < cfg.min_klines:\n            timeline.append({\n                'candle_idx': i,\n                'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n                'regime': 'unknown',\n                'adx': 0.0,\n                'sma_direction': 'flat',\n            })\n            continue\n\n        details = detector.detect_with_details(window)\n        adx = details['adx']\n        sma_dir = details['sma_direction']\n\n        # 滞后阈值（等价于 RegimeStrategy._apply_hysteresis）\n        if current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\"):\n            if adx < cfg.trend_exit_adx:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n        else:\n            if adx > cfg.trend_enter_adx:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # 禁止 bull↔bear 直接翻转\n        if (current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime != current_regime):\n            new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # min_dwell + confirm（等价于 RegimeStrategy._maybe_switch）\n        if new_regime == current_regime:\n            regime_bars += 1\n            pending_regime = None\n            pending_count = 0\n        elif regime_bars < cfg.min_dwell_bars:\n            regime_bars += 1\n        else:\n            if new_regime == pending_regime:\n                pending_count += 1\n            else:\n                pending_regime = new_regime\n                pending_count = 1\n\n            if pending_count >= cfg.confirm_bars:\n                current_regime = new_regime\n                regime_bars = 1\n                pending_regime = None\n                pending_count = 0\n            else:\n                regime_bars += 1\n\n        timeline.append({\n            'candle_idx': i,\n            'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n            'regime': current_regime,\n            'adx': adx,\n            'sma_direction': sma_dir,\n        })\n\n    return timeline\n\n\n# ==================== 交易配对 ====================\n\ndef classify_close_type(trade: Trade, capital: float) -> str:\n    \"\"\"判断平仓类型\"\"\"\n    ot = trade.order_type\n    if 'TTP' in ot:\n        return 'ttp'\n    if ot == 'LIQUIDATION':\n        return 'liquidation'\n    # 止损判断：pnl ≈ -capital（固定注码下 -capital = -initial*0.1 = -50）\n    if capital > 0 and abs(trade.pnl + capital) / capital < 0.05:\n        return 'stop_loss'\n    return 'signal'\n\n\ndef pair_trades(trades: List[Trade], candle_indices: List[int],\n                regime_timeline: List[Dict], start_idx: int,\n                leverage: float, is_last_combo: bool = False) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"将原始 Trade 列表配对为开仓→平仓交易\n\n    Args:\n        trades: 回测引擎输出的交易列表\n        candle_indices: 每笔交易对应的 K 线索引\n        regime_timeline: regime 时间线（按 candle_idx 索引）\n        start_idx: K 线的 start_idx（regime_timeline 的偏移）\n        leverage: 杠杆倍数\n        is_last_combo: 是否最后一组（调试用）\n\n    Returns:\n        配对交易列表\n    \"\"\"\n    # 构建 candle_idx → regime 查找表\n    regime_map = {}\n    for entry in regime_timeline:\n        regime_map[entry['candle_idx']] = entry['regime']\n\n    open_orders = {'BUY', 'SELL'}\n    close_orders = {'CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL', 'TTP_CLOSE_BUY', 'TTP_CLOSE_SELL', 'LIQUIDATION'}\n\n    open_trade = None\n    open_idx = None\n    paired = []\n\n    for k in range(len(trades)):\n        t = trades[k]\n        idx = candle_indices[k] if k < len(candle_indices) else 0\n\n        if t.order_type in open_orders:\n            open_trade = t\n            open_idx = idx\n\n        elif t.order_type in close_orders and open_trade is not None:\n            direction = 'long' if open_trade.order_type == 'BUY' else 'short'\n            holding = idx - open_idx if open_idx is not None else 0\n\n            # 判断平仓类型\n            if t.order_type in close_orders and k == len(trades) - 1:\n                # 最后一笔且不是 TTP/LIQUIDATION → 可能是 end_of_data\n                if t.order_type in ('CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL'):\n                    close_type = 'end_of_data'\n                else:\n                    close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n            else:\n                close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n\n            # R 值 = pnl / capital\n            r_value = t.pnl / open_trade.capital if open_trade.capital > 0 else 0.0\n\n            # 查找开仓时的 regime\n            regime = regime_map.get(open_idx, 'unknown')\n\n            paired.append({\n                'open_candle_idx': open_idx,\n                'close_candle_idx': idx,\n                'open_time': open_trade.time,\n                'close_time': t.time,\n                'holding_bars': holding,\n                'direction': direction,\n                'entry_price': open_trade.price,\n                'exit_price': t.price,\n                'capital': open_trade.capital,\n                'position_size': open_trade.capital * leverage,\n                'pnl': for t in closing if t.pnl < 0)\n    return gross_profit / abs(gross_loss) if gross_loss < 0 else 0.0\n\n\n# ==================== 数据库操作 ====================\n\ndef init_db(db_path: str) -> 线数据（完整文件，不截取）\"\"\"\n    data_file = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'historical', coin, f'{interval}.json')\n    if not os.path.exists(data_file):\n        return []\n    with open(data_file, 'r') as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\n\n# ==================== Regime 时间线计算 ====================\n\ndef compute_regime_timeline(candles: List[Dict], interval: str,\n                            days: int) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"计算每根 K 线的 regime 标签\n\n    复制 RegimeStrategy 的滞后逻辑（_apply_hysteresis + _maybe_switch），\n    但不实例化任何子策略。\n\n    Returns:\n        列表，每个元素 = {candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction}\n    \"\"\"\n    bars_per_day_map = {\n        '1m': 1440, '5m': 288, '15m': 96, '30m': 48,\n        '1h': 24, '2h': 12, '4h': 6, '1d': 1,\n    }\n    bars_per_day = RegimeDetectorConfig(adx_period=adx_period)\n    detector = MarketRegimeDetector(cfg)\n\n    MAX_WINDOW = 200\n\n    # 滞后状态\n    current_regime = \"unknown\"\n    regime_bars = 0\n    pending_regime = None\n    pending_count = 0\n\n    timeline = []\n\n    for i in range(start_idx, n):\n        window_start = max(0, i + 1 - MAX_WINDOW)\n        window = candles[window_start:i + 1]\n\n        if len(window) < cfg.min_klines:\n            timeline.append({\n                'candle_idx': i,\n                'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n                'regime': 'unknown',\n                'adx': 0.0,\n                'sma_direction': 'flat',\n            })\n            continue\n\n        details = detector.detect_with_details(window)\n        adx = details['adx']\n        sma_dir = details['sma_direction']\n\n        # 滞后阈值（等价于 RegimeStrategy._apply_hysteresis）\n        if current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\"):\n            if adx < cfg.trend_exit_adx:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n        else:\n            if adx > cfg.trend_enter_adx:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # 禁止 bull↔bear 直接翻转\n        if (current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime != current_regime):\n            new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # min_dwell + confirm（等价于 RegimeStrategy._maybe_switch）\n        if new_regime == current_regime:\n            regime_bars += 1\n            pending_regime = None\n            pending_count = 0\n        elif regime_bars < cfg.min_dwell_bars:\n            regime_bars += 1\n        else:\n            if new_regime == pending_regime:\n                pending_count += 1\n            else:\n                pending_regime = new_regime\n                pending_count = 1\n\n            if pending_count >= cfg.confirm_bars:\n                current_regime = new_regime\n                regime_bars = 1\n                pending_regime = None\n                pending_count = 0\n            else:\n                regime_bars += 1\n\n        timeline.append({\n            'candle_idx': i,\n            'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n            'regime': current_regime,\n            'adx': adx,\n            'sma_direction': sma_dir,\n        })\n\n    return timeline\n\n\n# ==================== 交易配对 ====================\n\ndef classify_close_type(trade: Trade, capital: float) -> str:\n    \"\"\"判断平仓类型\"\"\"\n    ot = trade.order_type\n    if 'TTP' in ot:\n        return 'ttp'\n    if ot == 'LIQUIDATION':\n        return 'liquidation'\n    # 止损判断：pnl ≈ -capital（固定注码下 -capital = -initial*0.1 = -50）\n    if capital > 0 and abs(trade.pnl + capital) / capital < 0.05:\n        return 'stop_loss'\n    return 'signal'\n\n\ndef pair_trades(trades: List[Trade], candle_indices: List[int],\n                regime_timeline: List[Dict], start_idx: int,\n                leverage: float, is_last_combo: bool = False) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"将原始 Trade 列表配对为开仓→平仓交易\n\n    Args:\n        trades: 回测引擎输出的交易列表\n        candle_indices: 每笔交易对应的 K 线索引\n        regime_timeline: regime 时间线（按 candle_idx 索引）\n        start_idx: K 线的 start_idx（regime_timeline 的偏移）\n        leverage: 杠杆倍数\n        is_last_combo: 是否最后一组（调试用）\n\n    Returns:\n        配对交易列表\n    \"\"\"\n    # 构建 candle_idx → regime 查找表\n    regime_map = {}\n    for entry in regime_timeline:\n        regime_map[entry['candle_idx']] = entry['regime']\n\n    open_orders = {'BUY', 'SELL'}\n    close_orders = {'CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL', 'TTP_CLOSE_BUY', 'TTP_CLOSE_SELL', 'LIQUIDATION'}\n\n    open_trade = None\n    open_idx = None\n    paired = []\n\n    for k in range(len(trades)):\n        t = trades[k]\n        idx = candle_indices[k] if k < len(candle_indices) else 0\n\n        if t.order_type in open_orders:\n            open_trade = t\n            open_idx = idx\n\n        elif t.order_type in close_orders and open_trade is not None:\n            direction = 'long' if open_trade.order_type == 'BUY' else 'short'\n            holding = idx - open_idx if open_idx is not None else 0\n\n            # 判断平仓类型\n            if t.order_type in close_orders and k == len(trades) - 1:\n                # 最后一笔且不是 TTP/LIQUIDATION → 可能是 end_of_data\n                if t.order_type in ('CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL'):\n                    close_type = 'end_of_data'\n                else:\n                    close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n            else:\n                close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n\n            # R 值 = pnl / capital\n            r_value = t.pnl / open_trade.capital if open_trade.capital > 0 else 0.0\n\n            # 查找开仓时的 regime\n            regime = regime_map.get(open_idx, 'unknown')\n\n            paired.append({\n                'open_candle_idx': open_idx,\n                'close_candle_idx': idx,\n                'open_time': open_trade.time,\n                'close_time': t.time,\n                'holding_bars': holding,\n                'direction': direction,\n                'entry_price': open_trade.price,\n                'exit_price': t.price,\n                'capital': open_trade.capital,\n                'position_size': open_trade.capital * leverage,\n                'pnl': t.pnl,\n                'r_value': round(r_value, 6),\n                'balance_after': t.balance,\n                'close_type': close_type,\n                'regime_at_open': regime,\n            })\n\n            open_trade = None\n            open_idx = None\n\n    return paired\n\n\n# ==================== 汇总指标计算 ====================\n\ndef calc_profit_factor(trades: List[Trade]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"计算盈利因子\"\"\"\n    closing = [t for t in trades if 'CLOSE' in t.order_type or 'TTP' in t.order_type]\n    gross_profit = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl > 0)\n    gross_loss = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl < 0)\n    return gross_profit / abs(gross_loss) if gross_loss < 0 else 0.0\n\n\n# ==================== 数据库操作 ====================\n\ndef init_db(db_path: str) -> check_combo_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str,\n                       coin: str, interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 combo 是否已存在（用于断点恢复）\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n 'seed_report.db')\n\n# ==================== 数据库 Schema ====================\n\nSCHEMA_SQL = \"\"\"\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS combo_summary (\n    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n    strategy close_type TEXT,\n    regime_at_open TEXT\n);\n\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS regime_timeline (\n    coin TEXT NOT NULL,\n    interval TEXT NOT NULL,\n    candle_idx INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    candle_time_ms INTEGER,\n    regime TEXT,\n    adx REAL,\n    sma_direction TEXT\n);\n\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS run_metadata (\n    key TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n    value TEXT\n);\n\nCREATE INDEX IF NOT candle_idx);\nCREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_cs ON combo_summary(strategy, coin, interval);\n\"\"\"\n\n\n# ==================== K 线加载 ====================\n\ndef load_candles(coin: str, interval: str) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"加载 K 线数据（完整文件，不截取）\"\"\"\n    data_file = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'historical', coin, f'{interval}.json')\n    if not os.path.exists(data_file):\n        return []\n    with open(data_file, 'r') as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\n\n# ==================== Regime 时间线计算 ====================\n\ndef compute_regime_timeline(candles: List[Dict], interval: str,\n                            days: int) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"计算每根 K 线的 regime 标签\n\n    复制 RegimeStrategy 的滞后逻辑（_apply_hysteresis + _maybe_switch），\n    但不实例化任何子策略。\n\n    Returns:\n        列表，每个元素 = {candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction}\n    \"\"\"\n    bars_per_day_map = {\n        '1m': 1440, '5m': 288, '15m': 96, '30m': 48,\n        '1h': 24, '2h': 12, '4h': 6, '1d': 1,\n    }\n    bars_per_day = bars_per_day_map.get(interval, 24)\n\n    n = len(candles)\n    start_idx = max(0, n - days * bars_per_day)\n\n    # 配置\n    adx_period = get_adx_period(interval)\n    cfg = RegimeDetectorConfig(adx_period=adx_period)\n    detector = MarketRegimeDetector(cfg)\n\n    MAX_WINDOW = 200\n\n    # 滞后状态\n    current_regime = \"unknown\"\n    regime_bars = 0\n    pending_regime = None\n    pending_count = 0\n\n    timeline = []\n\n    for i in range(start_idx, n):\n        window_start = max(0, i + 1 - MAX_WINDOW)\n        window = candles[window_start:i + 1]\n\n        if len(window) < cfg.min_klines:\n            timeline.append({\n                'candle_idx': i,\n                'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n                'regime': 'unknown',\n                'adx': 0.0,\n                'sma_direction': 'flat',\n            })\n            continue\n\n        details = detector.detect_with_details(window)\n        adx = details['adx']\n        sma_dir = details['sma_direction']\n\n        # 滞后阈值（等价于 RegimeStrategy._apply_hysteresis）\n        if current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\"):\n            if adx < cfg.trend_exit_adx:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n        else:\n            if adx > cfg.trend_enter_adx:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # 禁止 bull↔bear 直接翻转\n        if (current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime != current_regime):\n            new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # min_dwell + confirm（等价于 RegimeStrategy._maybe_switch）\n        if new_regime == current_regime:\n            regime_bars += 1\n            pending_regime = None\n            pending_count = 0\n        elif regime_bars < cfg.min_dwell_bars:\n            regime_bars += 1\n        else:\n            if new_regime == pending_regime:\n                pending_count += 1\n            else:\n                pending_regime = new_regime\n                pending_count = 1\n\n            if pending_count >= cfg.confirm_bars:\n                current_regime = new_regime\n                regime_bars = 1\n                pending_regime = None\n                pending_count = 0\n            else:\n                regime_bars += 1\n\n        timeline.append({\n            'candle_idx': i,\n            'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n            'regime': current_regime,\n            'adx': adx,\n            'sma_direction': sma_dir,\n        })\n\n    return timeline\n\n\n# ==================== 交易配对 ====================\n\ndef classify_close_type(trade: Trade, capital: float) -> str:\n    \"\"\"判断平仓类型\"\"\"\n    ot = trade.order_type\n    if 'TTP' in ot:\n        return 'ttp'\n    if ot == 'LIQUIDATION':\n        return 'liquidation'\n    # 止损判断：pnl ≈ -capital（固定注码下 -capital = -initial*0.1 = -50）\n    if capital > 0 and abs(trade.pnl + capital) / capital < 0.05:\n        return 'stop_loss'\n    return 'signal'\n\n\ndef pair_trades(trades: List[Trade], candle_indices: List[int],\n                regime_timeline: List[Dict], start_idx: int,\n                leverage: float, is_last_combo: bool = False) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"将原始 Trade 列表配对为开仓→平仓交易\n\n    Args:\n        trades: 回测引擎输出的交易列表\n        candle_indices: 每笔交易对应的 K 线索引\n        regime_timeline: regime 时间线（按 candle_idx 索引）\n        start_idx: K 线的 start_idx（regime_timeline 的偏移）\n        leverage: 杠杆倍数\n        is_last_combo: 是否最后一组（调试用）\n\n    Returns:\n        配对交易列表\n    \"\"\"\n    # 构建 candle_idx → regime 查找表\n    regime_map = {}\n    for entry in regime_timeline:\n        regime_map[entry['candle_idx']] = entry['regime']\n\n    open_orders = {'BUY', 'SELL'}\n    close_orders = {'CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL', 'TTP_CLOSE_BUY', 'TTP_CLOSE_SELL', 'LIQUIDATION'}\n\n    open_trade = None\n    open_idx = None\n    paired = []\n\n    for k in range(len(trades)):\n        t = trades[k]\n        idx = candle_indices[k] if k < len(candle_indices) else 0\n\n        if t.order_type in open_orders:\n            open_trade = t\n            open_idx = idx\n\n        elif t.order_type in close_orders and open_trade is not None:\n            direction = 'long' if open_trade.order_type == 'BUY' else 'short'\n            holding = idx - open_idx if open_idx is not None else 0\n\n            # 判断平仓类型\n            if t.order_type in close_orders and k == len(trades) - 1:\n                # 最后一笔且不是 TTP/LIQUIDATION → 可能是 end_of_data\n                if t.order_type in ('CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL'):\n                    close_type = 'end_of_data'\n                else:\n                    close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n            else:\n                close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n\n            # R 值 = pnl / capital\n            r_value = t.pnl / open_trade.capital if open_trade.capital > 0 else 0.0\n\n            # 查找开仓时的 regime\n            regime = regime_map.get(open_idx, 'unknown')\n\n            paired.append({\n                'open_candle_idx': open_idx,\n                'close_candle_idx': idx,\n                'open_time': open_trade.time,\n                'close_time': t.time,\n                'holding_bars': holding,\n                'direction': direction,\n                'entry_price': open_trade.price,\n                'exit_price': t.price,\n                'capital': open_trade.capital,\n                'position_size': open_trade.capital * leverage,\n                'pnl': t.pnl,\n                'r_value': round(r_value, 6),\n                'balance_after': t.balance,\n                'close_type': close_type,\n                'regime_at_open': regime,\n            })\n\n            open_trade = None\n            open_idx = None\n\n    return paired\n\n\n# ==================== 汇总指标计算 ====================\n\ndef calc_profit_factor(trades: List[Trade]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"计算盈利因子\"\"\"\n    closing = [t for t in trades if 'CLOSE' in t.order_type or 'TTP' in t.order_type]\n    gross_profit = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl > 0)\n    gross_loss = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl < 0)\n    return gross_profit / abs(gross_loss) if gross_loss < 0 else 0.0\n\n\n# ==================== 数据库操作 ====================\n\ndef init_db(db_path: str) -> check_combo_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str,\n                       coin: str, interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 combo 是否已存在（用于断点恢复）\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM combo_summary WHERE strategy=? AND interval=?\",\n        (strategy, coin, interval)\n    )\n    return cur.fetchone() is not None\n\n\ndef check_regime_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, coin: str,\n                        interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 regime timeline 是否已存在\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM regime_timeline WHERE coin=? \"(strategy, coin, interval, total_return, final_balance, \"\n        \"max_drawdown, sharpe_ratio, sortino_ratio, calmar_ratio, \"\n        \"total_trades, winning_trades, losing_trades, win_rate, save_metadata(conn: sqlite3.Connection, config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"写入运行元数据\"\"\"\n    for key, value in config.items():\n        conn.execute(\n            \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO run_metadata strategies = get_strategies()\n    total = len(strategies) * len(COINS) * len(INTERVALS)\n    n_regime = len(COINS) * len(INTERVALS)\n\n    print(\"=\" * 90)\n    print(\"  种子报告生成器\")\n    print(\" time.time()\n            all_candles = load_candles(coin, interval)\n            if not all_candles:\n                print(\"  [!] %s/%s: 数据不存在，跳过\" % (coin, interval))\n                idx += len(strategies)\n                failed += len(strategies)\n                continue\n\n            bars_per_day = bars_per_day_map.get(interval, 24)\n            n_candles = len(all_candles)\n            start_idx = max(0, n_candles - DAYS * bars_per_day)\n            load_time = time.time() - t0\n\n            # ── 2. 计算 regime 时间线（只计算一次） ──\n            t1 = time.time()\n            if AND interval=? ── 3. 对每个策略运行回测 ──\n            for strategy_name in strategies:\n                idx += 1\n\n                elapsed_total = time.time() - start_all\n                if idx > 1:\n                    effective = idx - skipped - failed\n                    avg_per = elapsed_total / max(effective, 1)\n                    remaining = total - idx\n                    eta = avg_per * remaining\n                    eta_str = \" | ETA %.0fmin\" % (eta / 60)\n                else:\n                    eta_str = \"\"\n\n                # 每个 (coin, interval) 提交一次\n            conn.commit()\n\n    elapsed_all = time.time() - start_all\n\n    # 更新元数据\n    save_metadata(conn, {\n        'end_time': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n        'elapsed_minutes': round(elapsed_all / 60, 1),\n        'total_combos': total,\n        'skipped': skipped,\n        'failed': failed,\n    })\n\n    # ── 汇总统计 ──\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 90)\n    print(\"  种子报告生成完成 (耗时 %.1f 分钟)\" % (elapsed_all / 60))\n    print(\"=\" * 90)\n\n    # 数据库统计\n    n_combos = conn.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM combo_summary\").fetchone()[0]\n    n_paired = conn.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM paired_trades\").fetchone()[0]\n    n_regime = conn.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM regime_timeline\").fetchone()[0]\n\n    print(\"  combo_summary:  %d 行\" % n_combos)\n    print(\"  paired_trades:  %d 行\" % n_paired)\n    print(\"  regime_timeline: %d 行\" % n_regime)\n    print(\"  跳过(已有): %d | 失败: %d\" % (skipped, failed))\n\n    # 文件大小\n    conn.close()\n    db_size = os.path.getsize(DB_PATH)\n    print(\"  数据库大小: %.1f MB\" % (db_size / 1024 / 1024))\n\n    # Regime 分布总览\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)\n    print(\"\\n  Regime 分布总览:\")\n    for row in conn.execute(\n            \"SELECT regime, COUNT(*) FROM regime_timeline GROUP BY regime ORDER BY regime\"):\n        print(\"    %-10s %d 条\" % (row[0], row[1]))\n\n    # load_candles(coin: str, interval: str) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"加载 K 线数据（完整文件，不截取）\"\"\"\n    data_file = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'historical', coin, f'{interval}.json')\n    if not os.path.exists(data_file):\n        return []\n    with open(data_file, 'r') as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\n\n# ==================== Regime 时间线计算 ====================\n\ndef compute_regime_timeline(candles: List[Dict], interval: str,\n                            days: int) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"计算每根 K 线的 regime 标签\n\n    复制 RegimeStrategy 的滞后逻辑（_apply_hysteresis + _maybe_switch），\n    但不实例化任何子策略。\n\n    Returns:\n        列表，每个元素 = {candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction}\n    \"\"\"\n    bars_per_day_map = {\n        '1m': 1440, '5m': 288, '15m': 96, '30m': 48,\n        '1h': 24, '2h': 12, '4h': 6, '1d': 1,\n    }\n    bars_per_day = bars_per_day_map.get(interval, 24)\n\n    n = len(candles)\n    start_idx = max(0, n - days * bars_per_day)\n\n    # 配置\n    adx_period = get_adx_period(interval)\n    cfg = RegimeDetectorConfig(adx_period=adx_period)\n    detector = MarketRegimeDetector(cfg)\n\n    MAX_WINDOW = 200\n\n    # 滞后状态\n    current_regime = \"unknown\"\n    regime_bars = 0\n    pending_regime = None\n    pending_count = 0\n\n    timeline = []\n\n    for i in range(start_idx, n):\n        window_start = max(0, i + 1 - MAX_WINDOW)\n        window = candles[window_start:i + 1]\n\n        # candle_idx 使用 0-based 相对索引，与 BacktestEngine 的索引对齐\n        # BacktestEngine 截取 candles[-days*bars_per_day:]，索引从 0 开始\n        rel_idx = i - start_idx\n\n        if len(window) < cfg.min_klines:\n            timeline.append({\n                'candle_idx': rel_idx,\n                'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n                'regime': 'unknown',\n                'adx': 0.0,\n                'sma_direction': 'flat',\n            })\n            continue\n\n        details = detector.detect_with_details(window)\n        adx = details['adx']\n        sma_dir = details['sma_direction']\n\n        # 滞后阈值（等价于 RegimeStrategy._apply_hysteresis）\n        if current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\"):\n            if adx < cfg.trend_exit_adx:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n        else:\n            if adx > cfg.trend_enter_adx:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # 禁止 bull↔bear 直接翻转\n        if (current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime != current_regime):\n            new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # min_dwell + confirm（等价于 RegimeStrategy._maybe_switch）\n        if new_regime == current_regime:\n            regime_bars += 1\n            pending_regime = None\n            pending_count = 0\n        elif regime_bars < cfg.min_dwell_bars:\n            regime_bars += 1\n        else:\n            if new_regime == pending_regime:\n                pending_count += 1\n            else:\n                pending_regime = new_regime\n                pending_count = 1\n\n            if pending_count >= cfg.confirm_bars:\n                current_regime = new_regime\n                regime_bars = 1\n                pending_regime = None\n                pending_count = 0\n            else:\n                regime_bars += 1\n\n        timeline.append({\n            'candle_idx': i,\n            'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n            'regime': current_regime,\n            'adx': adx,\n            'sma_direction': sma_dir,\n        })\n\n    return timeline\n\n\n# ==================== 交易配对 ====================\n\ndef classify_close_type(trade: Trade, capital: float) -> str:\n    \"\"\"判断平仓类型\"\"\"\n    ot = trade.order_type\n    if 'TTP' in ot:\n        return 'ttp'\n    if ot == 'LIQUIDATION':\n        return 'liquidation'\n    # 止损判断：pnl ≈ -capital（固定注码下 -capital = -initial*0.1 = -50）\n    if capital > 0 and abs(trade.pnl + capital) / capital < 0.05:\n        return 'stop_loss'\n    return 'signal'\n\n\ndef pair_trades(trades: List[Trade], candle_indices: List[int],\n                regime_timeline: List[Dict], start_idx: int,\n                leverage: float, is_last_combo: bool = False) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"将原始 Trade 列表配对为开仓→平仓交易\n\n    Args:\n        trades: 回测引擎输出的交易列表\n        candle_indices: 每笔交易对应的 K 线索引\n        regime_timeline: regime 时间线（按 candle_idx 索引）\n        start_idx: K 线的 start_idx（regime_timeline 的偏移）\n        leverage: 杠杆倍数\n        is_last_combo: 是否最后一组（调试用）\n\n    Returns:\n        配对交易列表\n    \"\"\"\n    # 构建 candle_idx → regime 查找表\n    regime_map = {}\n    for entry in regime_timeline:\n        regime_map[entry['candle_idx']] = entry['regime']\n\n    open_orders = {'BUY', 'SELL'}\n    close_orders = {'CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL', 'TTP_CLOSE_BUY', 'TTP_CLOSE_SELL', 'LIQUIDATION'}\n\n    open_trade = None\n    open_idx = None\n    paired = []\n\n    for k in range(len(trades)):\n        t = trades[k]\n        idx = candle_indices[k] if k < len(candle_indices) else 0\n\n        if t.order_type in open_orders:\n            open_trade = t\n            open_idx = idx\n\n        elif t.order_type in close_orders and open_trade is not None:\n            direction = 'long' if open_trade.order_type == 'BUY' else 'short'\n            holding = idx - open_idx if open_idx is not None else 0\n\n            # 判断平仓类型\n            if t.order_type in close_orders and k == len(trades) - 1:\n                # 最后一笔且不是 TTP/LIQUIDATION → 可能是 end_of_data\n                if t.order_type in ('CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL'):\n                    close_type = 'end_of_data'\n                else:\n                    close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n            else:\n                close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n\n            # R 值 = pnl / capital\n            r_value = t.pnl / open_trade.capital if open_trade.capital > 0 else 0.0\n\n            # 查找开仓时的 regime\n            regime = regime_map.get(open_idx, 'unknown')\n\n            paired.append({\n                'open_candle_idx': open_idx,\n                'close_candle_idx': idx,\n                'open_time': open_trade.time,\n                'close_time': t.time,\n                'holding_bars': holding,\n                'direction': direction,\n                'entry_price': open_trade.price,\n                'exit_price': t.price,\n                'capital': open_trade.capital,\n                'position_size': open_trade.capital * leverage,\n                'pnl': t.pnl,\n                'r_value': round(r_value, 6),\n                'balance_after': t.balance,\n                'close_type': close_type,\n                'regime_at_open': regime,\n            })\n\n            open_trade = None\n            open_idx = None\n\n    return paired\n\n\n# ==================== 汇总指标计算 ====================\n\ndef calc_profit_factor(trades: List[Trade]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"计算盈利因子\"\"\"\n    closing = [t for t in trades if 'CLOSE' in t.order_type or 'TTP' in t.order_type]\n    gross_profit = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl > 0)\n    gross_loss = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl < 0)\n    return gross_profit / abs(gross_loss) if gross_loss < 0 else 0.0\n\n\n# ==================== 数据库操作 ====================\n\ndef init_db(db_path: str) -> sqlite3.Connection:\n    \"\"\"初始化数据库\"\"\"\n    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(db_path), exist_ok=True)\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL\")\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL\")\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA cache_size=-64000\")  # 64MB 缓存\n    conn.executescript(SCHEMA_SQL)\n    conn.commit()\n    return conn\n\n\ndef check_combo_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str,\n                       coin: str, interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 combo 是否已存在（用于断点恢复）\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM combo_summary WHERE strategy=? AND coin=? AND interval=?\",\n        (strategy, coin, interval)\n    )\n    return cur.fetchone() is not None\n\n\ndef check_regime_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, coin: str,\n                        interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 regime timeline 是否已存在\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM regime_timeline WHERE coin=? AND interval=? LIMIT 1\",\n        (coin, interval)\n    )\n    return cur.fetchone() is not None\n\n\ndef save_regime_timeline(conn: sqlite3.Connection, coin: str,\n                         interval: str, timeline: List[Dict]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"批量写入 regime 时间线\"\"\"\n    conn.executemany(\n        \"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO regime_timeline \"\n        \"(coin, interval, candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction) \"\n        \"VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\",\n        [(coin, interval, e['candle_idx'], e['candle_time_ms'],\n          e['regime'], e['adx'], e['sma_direction'])\n         for e in timeline]\n    )\n\n\ndef save_combo(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str, coin: str,\n               interval: str, result, paired: List[Dict]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"写入一个 combo 的汇总 + 配对交易\"\"\"\n    profit_factor = calc_profit_factor(result.trades)\n    ttp_count = len([t for t in result.trades if 'TTP' in t.order_type])\n\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"INSERT INTO combo_summary \"\n        \"(strategy, coin, interval, total_return, final_balance, \"\n        \"max_drawdown, sharpe_ratio, sortino_ratio, calmar_ratio, \"\n        \"total_trades, winning_trades, losing_trades, win_rate, \"\n        \"avg_win_pct, avg_loss_pct, profit_factor, ttp_count, \"\n        \"double_count, fastest_double_days, avg_double_days, daily_open_positions) \"\n        \"VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)\",\n        (strategy, coin, interval,\n         result.total_return, result.final_balance,\n         result.max_drawdown, result.sharpe_ratio, conn.executemany(\n            \"INSERT INTO paired_trades \"\n            \"(combo_id, open_candle_idx, close_candle_idx, open_time, close_time, \"\n            \"holding_bars, direction, entry_price, exit_price, capital, position_size, \"\n            \"pnl, r_value, balance_after, close_type, regime_at_open) \"\n            \"VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)\",\n            [(combo_id, p['open_candle_idx'], p['close_candle_idx'],\n              p['open_time'], p['close_time'], p['holding_bars'],\n              p['direction'], p['entry_price'], p['exit_price'],\n              p['capital'], p['position_size'], p['pnl'], p['r_value'],\n              p['balance_after'], p['close_type'], p['regime_at_open'])\n             for p in paired]\n        )\n\n\ndef save_metadata(conn: sqlite3.Connection, config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"写入运行元数据\"\"\"\n    for key, value in config.items():\n        conn.execute(\n            \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO run_metadata (key, value) VALUES (?, ?)\",\n            (key, json.dumps(value) if not isinstance(value, str) else value)\n        )\n    conn.commit()\n\n\n# ==================== 主流程 ====================\n\ndef get_strategies() -> List[str]:\n    \"\"\"获取所有可用策略\"\"\"\n    all_names = sorted(list_strategies())\n    return [name for name in all_names if name not in SKIP_STRATEGIES]\n\n\ndef main():\n    strategies = get_strategies()\n    total = len(strategies) * len(COINS) * len(INTERVALS)\n    n_regime = len(COINS) * len(INTERVALS)\n\n    print(\"=\" * 90)\n    print(\"  种子报告生成器\")\n    print(\"  %d 策略 × %d 币种 × %d 周期 = %d 组回测\" % (\n        len(strategies), len(COINS), len(INTERVALS), total))\n    print(\"  + %d 组 regime 时间线\" % n_regime)\n    print(\"  参数：%d天 · $%d · %.0fx · 止损%.0f%% · TTP%s time.time()\n            all_candles = load_candles(coin, interval)\n            if not all_candles:\n                print(\"  [!] %s/%s: 数据不存在，跳过\" % (coin, interval))\n                idx += len(strategies)\n                failed += len(strategies)\n                continue\n\n            bars_per_day = bars_per_day_map.get(interval, 24)\n            n_candles = len(all_candles)\n            start_idx = max(0, n_candles - DAYS * bars_per_day)\n            load_time = time.time() - t0\n\n            # ── 2. 计算 regime 时间线（只计算一次） ──\n            t1 = time.time()\n            if check_regime_exists(conn, coin, interval):\n                # 从数据库读取已有的 regime timeline\n                cur = conn.execute(\n                    \"SELECT candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction \"\n                    \"FROM regime_timeline WHERE coin=? AND interval=? 线数据（完整文件，不截取）\"\"\"\n    data_file = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'historical', coin, f'{interval}.json')\n    if not os.path.exists(data_file):\n        return []\n    with open(data_file, 'r') as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\n\n# ==================== Regime 时间线计算 ====================\n\ndef compute_regime_timeline(candles: List[Dict], interval: str,\n                            days: int) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"计算每根 K 线的 regime 标签\n\n    复制 RegimeStrategy 的滞后逻辑（_apply_hysteresis + _maybe_switch），\n    但不实例化任何子策略。\n\n    Returns:\n        列表，每个元素 = {candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction}\n    \"\"\"\n    bars_per_day_map = {\n        '1m': 1440, '5m': 288, '15m': 96, '30m': 48,\n        '1h': 24, '2h': 12, '4h': 6, '1d': 1,\n    }\n    bars_per_day = bars_per_day_map.get(interval, 24)\n\n    n = len(candles)\n    start_idx = max(0, n - days * bars_per_day)\n\n    # 配置\n    adx_period = get_adx_period(interval)\n    cfg = RegimeDetectorConfig(adx_period=adx_period)\n    detector = MarketRegimeDetector(cfg)\n\n    MAX_WINDOW = 200\n\n    # 滞后状态\n    current_regime = \"unknown\"\n    regime_bars = 0\n    pending_regime = None\n    pending_count = 0\n\n    timeline = []\n\n    for i in range(start_idx, n):\n        window_start = max(0, i + 1 - MAX_WINDOW)\n        window = candles[window_start:i + 1]\n\n        # candle_idx 使用 0-based 相对索引，与 BacktestEngine 的索引对齐\n        # BacktestEngine 截取 candles[-days*bars_per_day:]，索引从 0 开始\n        rel_idx = i - start_idx\n\n        if len(window) < cfg.min_klines:\n            timeline.append({\n                'candle_idx': rel_idx,\n                'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n                'regime': 'unknown',\n                'adx': 0.0,\n                'sma_direction': 'flat',\n            })\n            continue\n\n        details = detector.detect_with_details(window)\n        adx = details['adx']\n        sma_dir = details['sma_direction']\n\n        # 滞后阈值（等价于 RegimeStrategy._apply_hysteresis）\n        if current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\"):\n            if adx < cfg.trend_exit_adx:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n        else:\n            if adx > cfg.trend_enter_adx:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # 禁止 bull↔bear 直接翻转\n        if (current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime != current_regime):\n            new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # min_dwell + confirm（等价于 RegimeStrategy._maybe_switch）\n        if new_regime == current_regime:\n            regime_bars += 1\n            pending_regime = None\n            pending_count = 0\n        elif regime_bars < cfg.min_dwell_bars:\n            regime_bars += 1\n        else:\n            if new_regime == pending_regime:\n                pending_count += 1\n            else:\n                pending_regime = new_regime\n                pending_count = 1\n\n            if pending_count >= cfg.confirm_bars:\n                current_regime = new_regime\n                regime_bars = 1\n                pending_regime = None\n                pending_count = 0\n            else:\n                regime_bars += 1\n\n        timeline.append({\n            'candle_idx': rel_idx,\n            'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n            'regime': current_regime,\n            'adx': adx,\n            'sma_direction': sma_dir,\n        })\n\n    return timeline\n\n\n# ==================== 交易配对 ====================\n\ndef classify_close_type(trade: Trade, capital: float) -> str:\n    \"\"\"判断平仓类型\"\"\"\n    ot = trade.order_type\n    if 'TTP' in ot:\n        return 'ttp'\n    if ot == 'LIQUIDATION':\n        return 'liquidation'\n    # 止损判断：pnl ≈ -capital（固定注码下 -capital = -initial*0.1 = -50）\n    if capital > 0 and abs(trade.pnl + capital) / capital < 0.05:\n        return 'stop_loss'\n    return 'signal'\n\n\ndef pair_trades(trades: List[Trade], candle_indices: List[int],\n                regime_timeline: List[Dict], start_idx: int,\n                leverage: float, is_last_combo: bool = False) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"将原始 Trade 列表配对为开仓→平仓交易\n\n    Args:\n        trades: 回测引擎输出的交易列表\n        candle_indices: 每笔交易对应的 K 线索引\n        regime_timeline: regime 时间线（按 candle_idx 索引）\n        start_idx: K 线的 start_idx（regime_timeline 的偏移）\n        leverage: 杠杆倍数\n        is_last_combo: 是否最后一组（调试用）\n\n    Returns:\n        配对交易列表\n    \"\"\"\n    # 构建 candle_idx → regime 查找表\n    regime_map = {}\n    for entry in regime_timeline:\n        regime_map[entry['candle_idx']] = entry['regime']\n\n    open_orders = {'BUY', 'SELL'}\n    close_orders = {'CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL', 'TTP_CLOSE_BUY', 'TTP_CLOSE_SELL', 'LIQUIDATION'}\n\n    open_trade = None\n    open_idx = None\n    paired = []\n\n    for k in range(len(trades)):\n        t = trades[k]\n        idx = candle_indices[k] if k < len(candle_indices) else 0\n\n        if t.order_type in open_orders:\n            open_trade = t\n            open_idx = idx\n\n        elif t.order_type in close_orders and open_trade is not None:\n            direction = 'long' if open_trade.order_type == 'BUY' else 'short'\n            holding = idx - open_idx if open_idx is not None else 0\n\n            # 判断平仓类型\n            if t.order_type in close_orders and k == len(trades) - 1:\n                # 最后一笔且不是 TTP/LIQUIDATION → 可能是 end_of_data\n                if t.order_type in ('CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL'):\n                    close_type = 'end_of_data'\n                else:\n                    close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n            else:\n                close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n\n            # R 值 = pnl / capital\n            r_value = t.pnl / open_trade.capital if open_trade.capital > 0 else 0.0\n\n            # 查找开仓时的 regime\n            regime = regime_map.get(open_idx, 'unknown')\n\n            paired.append({\n                'open_candle_idx': open_idx,\n                'close_candle_idx': idx,\n                'open_time': open_trade.time,\n                'close_time': t.time,\n                'holding_bars': holding,\n                'direction': direction,\n                'entry_price': open_trade.price,\n                'exit_price': t.price,\n                'capital': open_trade.capital,\n                'position_size': open_trade.capital * leverage,\n                'pnl': t.pnl,\n                'r_value': round(r_value, 6),\n                'balance_after': t.balance,\n                'close_type': close_type,\n                'regime_at_open': regime,\n            })\n\n            open_trade = None\n            open_idx = None\n\n    return paired\n\n\n# ==================== 汇总指标计算 ====================\n\ndef calc_profit_factor(trades: List[Trade]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"计算盈利因子\"\"\"\n    closing = [t for t in trades if 'CLOSE' in t.order_type or 'TTP' in t.order_type]\n    gross_profit = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl > 0)\n    gross_loss = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl < 0)\n    return gross_profit / abs(gross_loss) if gross_loss < 0 else 0.0\n\n\n# ==================== 数据库操作 ====================\n\ndef init_db(db_path: str) -> sqlite3.Connection:\n    \"\"\"初始化数据库\"\"\"\n    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(db_path), exist_ok=True)\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL\")\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL\")\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA cache_size=-64000\")  # 64MB 缓存\n    conn.executescript(SCHEMA_SQL)\n    conn.commit()\n    return conn\n\n\ndef check_combo_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str,\n                       coin: str, interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 combo 是否已存在（用于断点恢复）\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM combo_summary WHERE strategy=? AND coin=? AND interval=?\",\n        (strategy, coin, interval)\n    )\n    return cur.fetchone() is not None\n\n\ndef check_regime_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, coin: str,\n                        interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 regime timeline 是否已存在\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM regime_timeline WHERE coin=? AND interval=? LIMIT 1\",\n        (coin, interval)\n    )\n    return cur.fetchone() is not None\n\n\ndef save_regime_timeline(conn: sqlite3.Connection, coin: str,\n                         interval: str, timeline: List[Dict]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"批量写入 regime 时间线\"\"\"\n    conn.executemany(\n        \"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO regime_timeline \"\n        \"(coin, interval, candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction) \"\n        \"VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\",\n        [(coin, interval, e['candle_idx'], e['candle_time_ms'],\n          e['regime'], e['adx'], e['sma_direction'])\n         for e in timeline]\n    )\n\n\ndef save_combo(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str, coin: str,\n               interval: str, result, paired: List[Dict]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"写入一个 combo 的汇总 + 配对交易\"\"\"\n \"(strategy, coin, interval, total_return, final_balance, \"\n        \"max_drawdown, sharpe_ratio, sortino_ratio, calmar_ratio, \"\n        \"total_trades, winning_trades, losing_trades, win_rate, (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)\",\n        (strategy, coin, interval,\n         result.total_return, result.final_balance,\n         result.max_drawdown, result.sharpe_ratio, \"\"\"\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS combo_summary (\n    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n    strategy TEXT NOT NULL,\n    coin TEXT NOT NULL,\n    interval TEXT NOT NULL,\n    total_return 线数据（完整文件，不截取）\"\"\"\n    data_file = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'historical', coin, f'{interval}.json')\n    if not os.path.exists(data_file):\n        return []\n    with open(data_file, 'r') as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\n\n# ==================== Regime 时间线计算 ====================\n\ndef compute_regime_timeline(candles: List[Dict], interval: str,\n                            days: int) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"计算每根 K 线的 regime 标签\n\n    复制 RegimeStrategy 的滞后逻辑（_apply_hysteresis + _maybe_switch），\n    但不实例化任何子策略。\n\n    Returns:\n        列表，每个元素 = {candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction}\n    \"\"\"\n    bars_per_day_map = {\n        '1m': 1440, '5m': 288, '15m': 96, '30m': 48,\n        '1h': 24, '2h': 12, '4h': 6, '1d': 1,\n    }\n    bars_per_day = bars_per_day_map.get(interval, 24)\n\n    n = len(candles)\n    start_idx = max(0, n - days * bars_per_day)\n\n    # 配置\n    adx_period = get_adx_period(interval)\n    cfg = RegimeDetectorConfig(adx_period=adx_period)\n    detector = MarketRegimeDetector(cfg)\n\n    MAX_WINDOW = 200\n\n    # 滞后状态\n    current_regime = \"unknown\"\n    regime_bars = 0\n    pending_regime = None\n    pending_count = 0\n\n    timeline = []\n\n    for i in range(start_idx, n):\n        window_start = max(0, i + 1 - MAX_WINDOW)\n        window = candles[window_start:i + 1]\n\n        # candle_idx 使用 0-based 相对索引，与 BacktestEngine 的索引对齐\n        # BacktestEngine 截取 candles[-days*bars_per_day:]，索引从 0 开始\n        rel_idx = i - start_idx\n\n        if len(window) < cfg.min_klines:\n            timeline.append({\n                'candle_idx': rel_idx,\n                'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n                'regime': 'unknown',\n                'adx': 0.0,\n                'sma_direction': 'flat',\n            })\n            continue\n\n        details = detector.detect_with_details(window)\n        adx = details['adx']\n        sma_dir = details['sma_direction']\n\n        # 滞后阈值（等价于 RegimeStrategy._apply_hysteresis）\n        if current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\"):\n            if adx < cfg.trend_exit_adx:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n        else:\n            if adx > cfg.trend_enter_adx:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # 禁止 bull↔bear 直接翻转\n        if (current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime != current_regime):\n            new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # min_dwell + confirm（等价于 RegimeStrategy._maybe_switch）\n        if new_regime == current_regime:\n            regime_bars += 1\n            pending_regime = None\n            pending_count = 0\n        elif regime_bars < cfg.min_dwell_bars:\n            regime_bars += 1\n        else:\n            if new_regime == pending_regime:\n                pending_count += 1\n            else:\n                pending_regime = new_regime\n                pending_count = 1\n\n            if pending_count >= cfg.confirm_bars:\n                current_regime = new_regime\n                regime_bars = 1\n                pending_regime = None\n                pending_count = 0\n            else:\n                regime_bars += 1\n\n        timeline.append({\n            'candle_idx': rel_idx,\n            'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n            'regime': current_regime,\n            'adx': adx,\n            'sma_direction': sma_dir,\n        })\n\n    return timeline\n\n\n# ==================== 交易配对 ====================\n\ndef classify_close_type(trade: Trade, capital: float) -> str:\n    \"\"\"判断平仓类型\"\"\"\n    ot = trade.order_type\n    if 'TTP' in ot:\n        return 'ttp'\n    if ot == 'LIQUIDATION':\n        return 'liquidation'\n    # 止损判断：pnl ≈ -capital（固定注码下 -capital = -initial*0.1 = -50）\n    if capital > 0 and abs(trade.pnl + capital) / capital < 0.05:\n        return 'stop_loss'\n    return 'signal'\n\n\ndef pair_trades(trades: List[Trade], candle_indices: List[int],\n                regime_timeline: List[Dict],\n                leverage: float) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"将原始 Trade 列表配对为开仓→平仓交易\n\n    Args:\n        trades: 回测引擎输出的交易列表\n        candle_indices: 每笔交易对应的 K 线索引（0-based）\n        regime_timeline: regime 时间线（candle_idx 也是 0-based）\n        leverage: 杠杆倍数\n\n    Returns:\n        配对交易列表\n    \"\"\"\n    # 构建 candle_idx → regime 查找表\n    regime_map = {}\n    for entry in regime_timeline:\n        regime_map[entry['candle_idx']] = entry['regime']\n\n    open_orders = {'BUY', 'SELL'}\n    close_orders = {'CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL', 'TTP_CLOSE_BUY', 'TTP_CLOSE_SELL', 'LIQUIDATION'}\n\n    open_trade = None\n    open_idx = None\n    paired = []\n\n    for k in range(len(trades)):\n        t = trades[k]\n        idx = candle_indices[k] if k < len(candle_indices) else 0\n\n        if t.order_type in open_orders:\n            open_trade = t\n            open_idx = idx\n\n        elif t.order_type in close_orders and open_trade is not None:\n            direction = 'long' if open_trade.order_type == 'BUY' else 'short'\n            holding = idx - open_idx if open_idx is not None else 0\n\n            # 判断平仓类型\n            if t.order_type in close_orders and k == len(trades) - 1:\n                # 最后一笔且不是 TTP/LIQUIDATION → 可能是 end_of_data\n                if t.order_type in ('CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL'):\n                    close_type = 'end_of_data'\n                else:\n                    close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n            else:\n                close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n\n            # R 值 = pnl / capital\n            r_value = t.pnl / open_trade.capital if open_trade.capital > 0 else 0.0\n\n            # 查找开仓时的 regime\n            regime = regime_map.get(open_idx, 'unknown')\n\n            paired.append({\n                'open_candle_idx': open_idx,\n                'close_candle_idx': idx,\n                'open_time': open_trade.time,\n                'close_time': t.time,\n                'holding_bars': holding,\n                'direction': direction,\n                'entry_price': open_trade.price,\n                'exit_price': t.price,\n                'capital': open_trade.capital,\n                'position_size': open_trade.capital * leverage,\n                'pnl': t.pnl,\n                'r_value': round(r_value, 6),\n                'balance_after': t.balance,\n                'close_type': close_type,\n                'regime_at_open': regime,\n            })\n\n            open_trade = None\n            open_idx = None\n\n    return paired\n\n\n# ==================== 汇总指标计算 ====================\n\ndef calc_profit_factor(trades: List[Trade]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"计算盈利因子\"\"\"\n    closing = [t for t in trades if 'CLOSE' in t.order_type or 'TTP' in t.order_type]\n    gross_profit = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl > 0)\n    gross_loss = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl < 0)\n    return gross_profit / abs(gross_loss) if gross_loss < 0 else 0.0\n\n\n# ==================== 数据库操作 ====================\n\ndef init_db(db_path: str) -> sqlite3.Connection:\n    \"\"\"初始化数据库\"\"\"\n conn.execute(\"PRAGMA cache_size=-64000\")  # 64MB 缓存\n    conn.executescript(SCHEMA_SQL)\n    conn.commit()\n    return conn\n\n\ndef check_combo_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str,\n                       coin: str, interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 combo 是否已存在（用于断点恢复）\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM combo_summary WHERE strategy=? AND coin=? AND interval=?\",\n        (strategy, coin, interval)\n    )\n    return cur.fetchone() is not None\n\n\ndef check_regime_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, coin: str,\n                        interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 regime timeline 是否已存在\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM regime_timeline WHERE coin=? AND interval=? LIMIT 1\",\n        (coin, interval)\n    )\n    return cur.fetchone() is not None\n\n\ndef save_regime_timeline(conn: sqlite3.Connection, coin: str,\n                         interval: str, timeline: timeline]\n    )\n\n\ndef save_combo(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str, coin: str,\n               interval: str, result, paired: List[Dict]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"写入一个 combo 的汇总 + 配对交易\"\"\"\n    profit_factor = calc_profit_factor(result.trades)\n    ttp_count = len([t for t in result.trades if 'TTP' in t.order_type])\n\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"INSERT INTO combo_summary \"\n        \"(strategy, coin, interval, total_return, final_balance, \"\n        \"max_drawdown, sharpe_ratio, sortino_ratio, calmar_ratio, \"\n        \"total_trades, winning_trades, losing_trades, win_rate, \"\n        \"avg_win_pct, avg_loss_pct, profit_factor, ttp_count, \"\n        \"double_count, fastest_double_days, avg_double_days, daily_open_positions) \"\n        \"VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)\",\n        (strategy, coin, interval,\n         result.total_return, result.final_balance,\n         result.max_drawdown, result.sharpe_ratio, conn.executemany(\n            \"INSERT INTO paired_trades \"\n            \"(combo_id, open_candle_idx, close_candle_idx, open_time, close_time, \"\n            \"holding_bars, direction, [(combo_id, p['open_candle_idx'], p['close_candle_idx'],\n              p['open_time'], p['close_time'], p['holding_bars'],\n              p['direction'], p['entry_price'], p['exit_price'],\n              p['capital'], p['position_size'], p['pnl'], p['r_value'],\n              p['balance_after'], p['close_type'], p['regime_at_open'])\n             for p in paired]\n        )\n\n\ndef save_metadata(conn: sqlite3.Connection, config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"写入运行元数据\"\"\"\n    for key, value in config.items():\n        conn.execute(\n            \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO run_metadata 持仓 3 天 = 被收 9 次资金费\n    → 记录次数方便算真实成本\n```\n\n## Prop Firm 考核标准（以后申请用）\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  典型考核（搜索结果汇总）                  │\n│ │\n│                                         │\n│  关键发现:                               │\n│  控制在 4%日回撤 + 6%总回撤的人            │\n│  通过率高 75%                            │\n│                                         │\n│  稳定的 1-2%/周 >> 暴赚暴亏               │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## 最终字段清单\n\n```\nbacktest.py 改动：\n├── 手续费         → pnl 扣 taker fee\n├── 资金费率       → 每 N 根K线扣一次（按持仓时长）\n├── 滑点          → 成交价偏移 0.02%\n├── MFE/MAE       → 持仓期间追踪最高最低浮盈浮亏\n└── 时间戳精确化    → '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M'\n\npaired_trades 新增字段：\n├── fee            REAL    -- 手续费（开+平）\n├── funding_cost   REAL    -- 累计资金费\n├── slippage_cost  REAL    -- 滑点成本\n├── mfe            REAL    -- 最大浮盈\n├── mae            REAL    -- 最大浮亏\n├── open_atr_pct   REAL    -- 开仓时波动率\n├── open_volume    REAL    -- 开仓时成交量\n└── funding_count  INTEGER -- 经历几次资金费结算\n\ncombo_summary 新增字段：\n├── cagr           REAL    -- 年化复合增长率\n├── max_daily_dd   REAL    -- 最大单日回撤\n├── reward_risk    REAL    -- 盈亏比\n├── max_consec_loss_amt REAL -- 最大连续亏损金额\n└── total_fees     REAL    -- 总手续费+资金费+滑点\n```\n\n这样出来的种子就是**专业级**的，直接能用来准备 Prop Firm 考核。要不要全加？\n\nSources:\n- [Trading Performance ====================\n   347→\n   348→def calc_profit_factor(trades: List[Trade]) -> float:\n   349→    \"\"\"计算盈利因子\"\"\"\n   350→    closing = [t for t in trades if 'CLOSE' in t.order_type or 'TTP' 线数据（完整文件，不截取）\"\"\"\n    data_file = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'historical', coin, f'{interval}.json')\n    if not os.path.exists(data_file):\n        return []\n    with open(data_file, 'r') as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\n\n# ==================== Regime 时间线计算 ====================\n\ndef compute_regime_timeline(candles: List[Dict], interval: str,\n                            days: int) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"计算每根 K 线的 regime 标签\n\n    复制 RegimeStrategy 的滞后逻辑（_apply_hysteresis + _maybe_switch），\n    但不实例化任何子策略。\n\n    Returns:\n        列表，每个元素 = {candle_idx, candle_time_ms, regime, adx, sma_direction}\n    \"\"\"\n    bars_per_day_map = {\n        '1m': 1440, '5m': 288, '15m': 96, '30m': 48,\n        '1h': 24, '2h': 12, '4h': 6, '1d': 1,\n    }\n    bars_per_day = RegimeDetectorConfig(adx_period=adx_period)\n    detector = MarketRegimeDetector(cfg)\n\n    MAX_WINDOW = 200\n\n    # 滞后状态\n    current_regime = \"unknown\"\n    regime_bars = 0\n    pending_regime = None\n    pending_count = 0\n\n    timeline = []\n\n    for i in range(start_idx, n):\n        window_start = max(0, i + 1 - MAX_WINDOW)\n        window = candles[window_start:i + 1]\n\n        # candle_idx 使用 0-based 相对索引，与 BacktestEngine 的索引对齐\n        # BacktestEngine 截取 candles[-days*bars_per_day:]，索引从 0 开始\n        rel_idx = i - start_idx\n\n        if len(window) < cfg.min_klines:\n            timeline.append({\n                'candle_idx': rel_idx,\n                'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n                'regime': 'unknown',\n                'adx': 0.0,\n                'sma_direction': 'flat',\n            })\n            continue\n\n        details = detector.detect_with_details(window)\n        adx = details['adx']\n        sma_dir = details['sma_direction']\n\n        # 滞后阈值（等价于 RegimeStrategy._apply_hysteresis）\n        if current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\"):\n            if adx < cfg.trend_exit_adx:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n        else:\n            if adx > cfg.trend_enter_adx:\n                new_regime = \"bull\" if sma_dir == \"up\" else \"bear\"\n            else:\n                new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # 禁止 bull↔bear 直接翻转\n        if (current_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime in (\"bull\", \"bear\")\n                and new_regime != current_regime):\n            new_regime = \"ranging\"\n\n        # min_dwell + confirm（等价于 RegimeStrategy._maybe_switch）\n        if new_regime == current_regime:\n            regime_bars += 1\n            pending_regime = None\n            pending_count = 0\n        elif regime_bars < cfg.min_dwell_bars:\n            regime_bars += 1\n        else:\n            if new_regime == pending_regime:\n                pending_count += 1\n            else:\n                pending_regime = new_regime\n                pending_count = 1\n\n            if pending_count >= cfg.confirm_bars:\n                current_regime = new_regime\n                regime_bars = 1\n                pending_regime = None\n                pending_count = 0\n            else:\n                regime_bars += 1\n\n        timeline.append({\n            'candle_idx': rel_idx,\n            'candle_time_ms': candles[i].get('timestamp', candles[i].get('time', 0)),\n            'regime': current_regime,\n            'adx': adx,\n            'sma_direction': sma_dir,\n        })\n\n    return timeline\n\n\n# ==================== 交易配对 ====================\n\ndef classify_close_type(trade: Trade, capital: float) -> str:\n    \"\"\"判断平仓类型\"\"\"\n    ot = trade.order_type\n    if 'TTP' in ot:\n        return 'ttp'\n    if ot == 'LIQUIDATION':\n        return 'liquidation'\n    # 止损判断：pnl ≈ -capital（固定注码下 -capital = -initial*0.1 = -50）\n    if capital > 0 and abs(trade.pnl + capital) / capital < 0.05:\n        return 'stop_loss'\n    return 'signal'\n\n\ndef pair_trades(trades: List[Trade], candle_indices: List[int],\n                regime_timeline: List[Dict],\n                leverage: float) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"将原始 Trade 列表配对为开仓→平仓交易\n\n    Args:\n        trades: 回测引擎输出的交易列表\n        candle_indices: 每笔交易对应的 K 线索引（0-based）\n        regime_timeline: regime 时间线（candle_idx 也是 0-based）\n        leverage: 杠杆倍数\n\n    Returns:\n        配对交易列表\n    \"\"\"\n    # 构建 candle_idx → regime 查找表\n    regime_map = {}\n    for entry in regime_timeline:\n        regime_map[entry['candle_idx']] = entry['regime']\n\n    open_orders = {'BUY', 'SELL'}\n    close_orders = {'CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL', 'TTP_CLOSE_BUY', 'TTP_CLOSE_SELL', 'LIQUIDATION'}\n\n    open_trade = None\n    open_idx = None\n    paired = []\n\n    for k in range(len(trades)):\n        t = trades[k]\n        idx = candle_indices[k] if k < len(candle_indices) else 0\n\n        if t.order_type in open_orders:\n            open_trade = t\n            open_idx = idx\n\n        elif t.order_type in close_orders and open_trade is not None:\n            direction = 'long' if open_trade.order_type == 'BUY' else 'short'\n            holding = idx - open_idx if open_idx is not None else 0\n\n            # 判断平仓类型\n            if t.order_type in close_orders and k == len(trades) - 1:\n                # 最后一笔且不是 TTP/LIQUIDATION → 可能是 end_of_data\n                if t.order_type in ('CLOSE_BUY', 'CLOSE_SELL'):\n                    close_type = 'end_of_data'\n                else:\n                    close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n            else:\n                close_type = classify_close_type(t, open_trade.capital)\n\n            # R 值 = pnl / capital\n            r_value = t.pnl / open_trade.capital if open_trade.capital > 0 else 0.0\n\n            # 查找开仓时的 regime\n            regime = regime_map.get(open_idx, 'unknown')\n\n            paired.append({\n                'open_candle_idx': open_idx,\n                'close_candle_idx': idx,\n                'open_time': open_trade.time,\n                'close_time': t.time,\n                'holding_bars': holding,\n                'direction': direction,\n                'entry_price': open_trade.price,\n                'exit_price': t.price,\n                'capital': open_trade.capital,\n                'position_size': open_trade.capital * leverage,\n                'pnl': t.pnl,\n                'r_value': round(r_value, 6),\n                'balance_after': t.balance,\n                'close_type': close_type,\n                'regime_at_open': regime,\n            })\n\n            open_trade = None\n            open_idx = None\n\n    return paired\n\n\n# ==================== 汇总指标计算 ====================\n\ndef calc_profit_factor(trades: List[Trade]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"计算盈利因子\"\"\"\n    closing = [t for t in trades if 'CLOSE' in t.order_type or 'TTP' in t.order_type]\n    gross_profit = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl > 0)\n    gross_loss = sum(t.pnl for t in closing if t.pnl < 0)\n    return gross_profit / abs(gross_loss) if gross_loss < 0 else 0.0\n\n\n# ==================== 数据库操作 ====================\n\ndef init_db(db_path: str) -> sqlite3.Connection:\n    \"\"\"初始化数据库\"\"\"\n    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(db_path), exist_ok=True)\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL\")\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL\")\n    conn.execute(\"PRAGMA cache_size=-64000\")  # 64MB 缓存\n    conn.executescript(SCHEMA_SQL)\n    conn.commit()\n    return conn\n\n\ndef check_combo_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str,\n                       coin: str, interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 combo 是否已存在（用于断点恢复）\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM combo_summary WHERE strategy=? AND coin=? AND interval=?\",\n        (strategy, coin, interval)\n    )\n    return cur.fetchone() is not None\n\n\ndef check_regime_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, coin: str,\n                        interval: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"检查 regime timeline 是否已存在\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"SELECT 1 FROM regime_timeline WHERE coin=? AND interval=? timeline]\n    )\n\n\ndef save_combo(conn: sqlite3.Connection, strategy: str, coin: str,\n               interval: str, result, paired: List[Dict]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"写入一个 combo 的汇总 + 配对交易\"\"\"\n    profit_factor = calc_profit_factor(result.trades)\n    ttp_count = len([t for t in result.trades if 'TTP' in t.order_type])\n\n    cur = conn.execute(\n        \"INSERT INTO combo_summary \"\n
